PACKAGER:
                  All parts of a plant of the genus cannabis, whether growing or not; the seeds of
                  a plant of that type; the resin extracted from a part of a plant of that type;
                  and every compound, manufacture, salt, derivative, mixture, or preparation of a
                  plant of that type or of its seeds or resin. "Marijuana" does not include the
                  mature stalks of the plant or fiber produced from the stalks; oil or cake made
MARIJUANA:        from the seeds of the plant; or any other compound, manufacture, salt,
                  derivative, mixture, or preparation of the mature stalks, except the resin
                  extracted from the mature stalks, fiber, oil or cake; the sterilized seed of the

                  Cannabis sativa L. and any part of such plant, whether growing or not, with a
                  delta-9 tetrahydrocannabinol concentration of not more than three-tenths of one
                  percent (0.3%) on a dry weight basis.
MEDICAL           Marijuana that is grown, processed, dispensed, tested, possessed, or used for a
MARIJUANA:        medical purpose, and includes medical marijuana concentrate and medical
                  marijuana products.

CONCENTRATE       plant by physical or chemical means, so as to deliver a product with a
("CONCENTRATE"):  cannabinoid concentration greater than the raw plant material from which it is
                  derived.

PRODUCT:          for administration to a qualified patient, including but not limited to oils,
                  tinctures, edibles, pills, topical forms, gels, creams, and other derivative
                  forms.
                  Unused, surplus, returned or out-of-date marijuana; recalled marijuana; unused
MEDICAL MARIJUANA marijuana; plant debris of the plant of the genus cannabis, including dead
WASTE:            plants and all unused plant parts and roots; and any wastewater generated during

CHAPTER 2
MEDICAL MARIJUANA ESTABLISHMENTS
SECTION:
18-201: Municipal Licenses
18-202: Zoning Requirements
18-203: Conditions Of Operations
18-204: Marijuana Growing Facilities For Personal Medical Use; Security
18-201: MUNICIPAL LICENSES:
   A.   All Commercial Marijuana Growers, Commercial Marijuana Processors,
Commercial Marijuana Transporters, Retail Marijuana Dispensaries, Licensed
Packagers, Wholesale Facilities, and Research Facilities are required to obtain
a permit from the City Clerk or their designee. These Commercial Establishments
are defined as any medical marijuana establishment licensed by the State of
Oklahoma. The Permit shall be issued by the City upon:
      1.   the Applicant's presentation of proof and verification of the
Applicant's current and valid License from the State Department pursuant to 63
O.S. § 420A et seq. and Title 310 of the Rules of the Oklahoma State Department
of Health: 681-1 et seq.; and
      2.   payment of the Permit Fee.
   B.   The City Commission will establish by resolution a fee to obtain the
Permit for each of the above described entities. The fee shall be used to
offset municipal expenses covering costs related to licensing, inspection,
administration and enforcement of the above described entities. (Ord. 483, 8-
12-2019)
18-202: ZONING REQUIREMENTS:
   A.   The following Commercial Establishments shall be located and subject to
the following zoning restrictions, pursuant to the City of Prague, Oklahoma
Zoning Ordinance, being
Section 12 of the Prague Municipal Code, effective 2-14-2000:
      1.   Commercial Marijuana Processors shall be located in areas zoned C-2
[General Commercial], I-1 [Light Industrial], or I-2 [Heavy Industrial];
      2.   Commercial Marijuana Growers (limited to indoor growing only) shall
be located in areas zoned C-2 [General Commercial], I-1 [Light Industrial], or
I-2 [Heavy Industrial];
      3.   Retail Marijuana Dispensaries shall be located in areas zoned C-1
[Light Commercial], C-2 [General Commercial], I-1 [Light Industrial], and I-2
[Heavy Industrial];
      4.   Commercial Marijuana Research Facilities may be located in areas
zoned C-1 [Light Commercial], C-2 [General Commercial], I-1 [Light Industrial],
and I-2 [Heavy Industrial];
      5.   Commercial Marijuana Growers (outdoor or indoor) shall be located in
areas zoned A [Agricultural], I-1 [Light Industrial], and I-2 [Heavy
Industrial];
      6.   Licensed Packagers, and Wholesale Facilities shall be located in
areas zoned I-1 [Light Industrial], and I-2 [Heavy Industrial];
      7.   All Commercial Establishments shall be prohibited from being located
in areas zoned R-1 [Single Family Residential], except Marijuana Growing
Facilities for Personal Medical Use, which shall be located in areas zoned R-1;
      8.   All Commercial Establishments shall be prohibited from being located
in areas zoned PUD [Planned Unit Development], except Commercial Marijuana
Dispensaries, which may be located in a PUD.
   B.   A Permit will not be granted to any Applicant where the proposed
location of the Retail/Dispensary Establishment would be located within one
thousand (1,000) feet of any public or private school entrance. (Ord. 483, 8-
12-2019)
18-203: CONDITIONS OF OPERATIONS:
   A.   Buildings or transportation vehicles where marijuana is stored or
dispensed must be equipped with ventilation/air filtration systems so that no
odors are detectable off premises.
   B.   Any growing area including any lighting, plumbing or electrical
components in use shall comply with municipal building and fire codes.
   C.   Any violations of this section will result in the revocation of the
permit, and a fine of $200.00 per day while the violation exists.
   D.   Nothing in this Ordinance shall be construed to: (1) allow persons to
engage in conduct that endangers or causes a public nuisance; or (2) allow any
activity that is otherwise illegal and not permitted by state law; in
particular, the above municipal regulations in this section are intended to
comport with, follow, but not exceed, those state regulations promulgated in 63
O.S. 420A et seq. and OAC 310-681-1 et seq. (Ord. 483, 8-12-2019)
18-204: MARIJUANA GROWING FACILITIES FOR PERSONAL MEDICAL USE; SECURITY:
   A.   Growing marijuana for personal medical use shall not be conducted in a
manner that constitutes a public nuisance. A public nuisance may be deemed to
exist if growing marijuana produces light, glare, heat, noise, odor or
vibration that is detrimental to public health, safety or welfare or interferes
with the reasonable enjoyment of life and property.
   B.   The primary use of the residential property in which marijuana is grown
shall remain at all times a residence, with legal and functioning cooking,
eating, sleeping and sanitation/bathing facilities with proper ingress and
egress. No room shall be used for growing marijuana where such cultivation will
impair or prevent the primary uses of cooking, eating, sleeping or sanitation/
bathing.
   C.   The above municipal regulations in this section are intended to comport
with, follow, but not exceed, those state regulations promulgated in 63 O.S.
420A et seq. and OAC 310-681-1 et seq. (Ord. 483, 8-12-2019)
